# Y

[Back to index](index.md)

## ya

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `YA`
- **Part of speech:** particle
- **Definition:** question
- **Register/status:** grammar; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** grammatical particle: mood
- **Example:** Ya ta mar?
- **Corpus:** active (4 attestations); tracks: daily-dialogues, literary-poetic; examples in daily-726, poetic-503

### Sense 2: particle

- **Pronunciation:** `YA`
- **Part of speech:** particle:mood
- **Definition:** question
- **Register/status:** mood; accepted
- **Domains:** daily-life
- **Literal:** Marks a direct question without changing word order.
- **Example:** Ya ta mar?
- **Corpus:** active (4 attestations); tracks: daily-dialogues, literary-poetic; examples in daily-726, poetic-503

## yab

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `YAB`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to animal, move as creature, or keep living creature
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** nature-ecology, travel-place, science-math
- **Root family:** `YB`; Nature; animal, creature, nonhuman life; animal, creature, moving nonhuman life
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** Y-B root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na yab.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

- **Pronunciation:** `YAMAG-RET`
- **Part of speech:** noun
- **Definition:** right, claim, or protected standing concerning: image, visual form
- **Register/status:** civic; accepted
- **Domains:** ritual-spiritual, art-beauty
- **Root family:** `YMG`; Ritual/poetry; image, visual form; image, visual form, seen representation
- **Pattern:** right
- **Literal:** Y-M-G root, right suffix -ret
- **Example:** Yamag-ret ret cel sak.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)
